III. Implicit Comparison with 比较 bǐjiào

Function: Function:

今天比较热。 Jīntiān bǐjiào rè. Today is relatively hot.

这家越南餐厅很远。 Zhè jiā yuènán cāntīng hěn yuǎn. This Vietnamese restaurant is very far.

坐地铁会比较快。 Zuò dìtiě huì bǐjiào kuài. Taking the MRT would be faster.

我们家姐姐会做饭。 Wǒmen jiā jiějie huì zuò fàn. In our family, my elder sister cooks better.

Structures: Structures:

否定 Negation: 否定 Negation:

昨天不热。 Zuótiān bù rè. Yesterday was not hot.

他不喜欢游泳。 Tā bù xǐhuān yóuyǒng. He doesn't like swimming as much (compared to some other activity or to someone else).

我最近比较忙。 Wǒ zuìjìn bǐjiào máng. I have been relatively busy lately.

Questions: Questions:

咖啡还是茶，你比较喜欢喝咖啡吗？ Kāfēi háishì chá, nǐ bǐjiào xǐhuān hē kāfēi ma? Coffee or tea, do you prefer drinking coffee?

你和哥哥，你比较会打棒球吗？ Nǐ hé gēge, nǐ bǐjiào huì dǎ bàngqiú ma? Between you and your older brother, do you play baseball better?

他宁愿去看美国电影还是日本电影？ Tā nìngyuàn qù kàn Měiguó diànyǐng háishì Rìběn diànyǐng? Would he prefer to go watch an American movie or a Japanese movie?

IV.

又...又... (yòu...yòu...) both...and...

Function: Function:

这家餐厅的菜又便宜又好吃，所以我们常来吃。 Zhè jiā cāntīng de cài yòu piányí yòu hǎochī, suǒyǐ wǒmen cháng lái chī. The food in this restaurant is both inexpensive and delicious, so we often eat here.

坐高铁又快又舒服，但是有点贵。 Zuò gāotiě yòu kuài yòu shūfú, dànshì yǒudiǎn guì. Taking the High Speed Rail is both fast and comfortable, but it's a little expensive.

我想喝茶又想喝咖啡，但是这里没有便利店。 Wǒ xiǎng hē chá yòu xiǎng hē kāfēi, dànshì zhèlǐ méiyǒu biànlì diàn. I want to drink both tea and coffee, but there are no convenience stores here.

Structures: Structures:

否定 Negation: 否定 Negation:

这个摊位做的臭豆腐有不臭又不辣。 Wǒ de jiù shòu yǒu bù chòu yòu bù là. The stinky tofu that the vendor made today tastes neither stinky nor spicy. 我觉得不好吃。 Wǒ juéde bù hǎochī. I don't think it tastes any good.

我的旧手机不能照相又不能上网。我想买一个新的。 Wǒ de jiù shǒujī bù néng zhàoxiàng yòu bù néng shàngwǎng. Wǒ xiǎng mǎi yīgè xīn de. My old cellphone cannot take photos, nor can it go online. I want to buy a new one.

当人们旅行或回到家乡时，他们会购买当地产品作为给朋友和家人的礼物。这是中国文化和传统的一部分。为了促进旅游业，台湾的地方政府鼓励销售展示特殊地方特色的物品，例如独特的食品和服装，这可以帮助提振当地经济。受欢迎的纪念品包括各种甜点和零食、农产品、海鲜、矿产以及具有历史意义的物品，例如阿里山茶、凤梨酥、太阳饼、花莲大理石、台湾珊瑚以及印有台湾图案的T恤和钥匙扣。

YouBike in Taipei

110

YouBike is Taipei's public bicycle rental system. The unmanned system is managed digitally and is available 24 hours a day. YouBike leverages the facts that bikes are eco-friendly, cost-effective, and a convenient way to connect between different modes of transport to encourage the public to drive less and use public transportation more.

A YouBike rental system in Taipei

Ask for renting bicycles

Notes on Pinyin and Pronunciation:
Pinyin Rules
When the vowel "i" is followed by "ang" but is not preceded by a consonant, the "i" is changed to "y." When "i" is followed by "eng" and is not preceded by a consonant, the "e" is omitted to become "ying".

I. Time-When vs. Time-Duration
功能: 时间-何时表达是指示动作发生或情况发生的词语或短语。它们指的是一个特定的时间点，例如早上6:30。时间-持续表达则指一段时间，例如几个小时。请参考以下例子。

注：年(nián), year; 礼拜(lǐ bài), week。

V. Condition Consequence 要是 yàoshi 就 jiù
．
Function: In this pattern, 要是 presents the condition, while 就 in the second clause presents the consequence.
要是我有钱，我就买大房子。
我要是不回国，我就跟你们一起去玩。
要是我有空，我就跟朋友一起去KTV唱歌。LESSON • 9 • 放假去哪裡玩？
Where will you go for the holidays?
Structures: 要是 (yào shì) is a conjunction, which can be placed before or after the subject of the first clause. In the second clause, 就 (jiù) is an adverb and is placed at the very beginning of the predicate.
你要是星期日有空，你就跟我去旅行吧！
If you are free on Sunday, then let's travel together!
要是下個月不忙，她就回國。
If she is not busy next month, then she will go back to her country.
你要是沒空，我們就不要去逛夜市。
If you are not free, then we won't go to the night market.

Subtitled Television Programs

With the exception of news, all television programs in Taiwan come with subtitles and there is no option to remove them. Taiwanese are accustomed to watching television or movies with subtitles, which make comprehending programs easier.

There are a few general explanations as to why programs come with subtitles. One understanding is that with the subtitles, the hearing-impaired can also understand programs. Another explanation is that since there are many dialects spoken in Taiwan and accents in Mandarin vary among people and places, subtitles help people understand the programs better as the written language is the same across all Chinese dialects. The third rationale is that since Chinese is a tonal language with different tones having different meanings, when words are placed together, their tones can be affected. Therefore, it is very likely that words with the same sounds can cause misinterpretation.

Furthermore, Chinese is not an alphabetic language and the connection between words and sounds is not as strong. Visualizing the words and hearing the sounds make it easier to understand what is being said. For example, if one hears the phrase "基隆是雨港" (Jīlóng shì yǔ gǎng) without seeing the characters, it is possible that the phrase could be understood as "基隆是漁港" (Jīlóng shì yú gǎng). With subtitles, misunderstandings like these can be eliminated.

節目畫面提供: udn TV• 當代中文課程的目標是教授學生使用時間表達事件，以及與朋友討論旅行計劃、談論假設情況和提供關於休閒活動的建議。第十課：台灣的水果外貌很好吃

學習目標：
- 學習簡單描述人的外貌。
- 學習描述食物的顏色、味道和口感。
- 學習簡要解釋並給出理由。
- 學習描述臨時活動和可變狀態。丶10-1
The Fruit in Taiwan Tastes Really Good.

妒王：這個黃色的水果叫什麼？
月其：芒果。給你一塊，吃吃看。
知王：好，謝謝。[taking a bite] 香香的、甜甜的，很好吃。
月其：昨天明華給我們的那種水果，紅色的，叫什麼？
知王：你說的是西瓜吧？
月其：對！對！對！台灣有很多好吃的水果。
知王：我以前不喜歡吃水果，現在很喜歡了。
月其：越南的水果也很好吃。
知王：要是有機會，我想吃吃看。
月其：妳來越南，我一定請妳吃。

Translation:
Dù Wáng: What is this yellow fruit called?
Yuè Qí: Mango. Here, have a piece and try it.
Zhī Wáng: Okay, thank you. [taking a bite] It's fragrant and sweet, very delicious.
Yuè Qí: The fruit that Minghua gave us yesterday, the red one, what is it called?
Zhī Wáng: Are you talking about watermelon?
Yuè Qí: Yes! Yes! Yes! Taiwan has many delicious fruits.
Zhī Wáng: I used to not like eating fruits, but now I really like them.
Yuè Qí: Vietnamese fruits are also very delicious.
Zhī Wáng: If there's a chance, I would like to try them.
Yuè Qí: If you come to Vietnam, I will definitely treat you to some.．咄皙一泊，
如並：這個黃色的水果是什麼？
月美：芒果。給你一塊吃吃看。
如洒：好，謝謝。香香的，甜甜的，味道不錯。
月美：昨天明華給我們的種水果，紅色的，叫什麼？
如洒：你說的是西瓜吧？
月美：對！就是它！台灣有很多好吃的水果。
如洒：過去我不喜歡吃水果，現在喜歡了。
月美：越南的水果也很好吃。
如洒：如果有機會，我想試試看。
月美：如果你來越南，我一定請你吃。• 當代中文課程生詞- Vocabulary I 10-2

The fruit in Taiwan tastes really good.

明华：你跟你女朋友上个月去花蓮玩，好玩吗？
中：很好玩。你看，这些是我拍的照片。
明华：你们笑得很开心！哪一个是你女朋友？
田中：穿红衣服的这个。穿黄衣服的是旅馆老板的太太。
明华：她们两个都很漂亮。这两个男的是谁？
田中：矮的是旅馆的老板，高的是他弟弟。
明华：那家旅馆怎么样？
田中：很干净。从窗户往外看，是蓝色的大海。
明华：真不错！那家旅馆贵吗？
中：因为现在去玩的人比较少，所以旅馆不太贵。
明华：下次我也想去住。

(Note: The pinyin with missing tones has been left as is, as it is not possible to determine the correct tones without context.)• 当代中文课程

明华：下次我也想去住。Lesson 10: 台灣的水果很好吃 (Táiwān de shuǐguǒ hěn hǎochī)
The fruit in Taiwan is very delicious.

Vocabulary:
1. 拍照 (pāizhào) - to take pictures
2. 笑 (xiào) - to laugh, to smile
3. 開心 (kāixīn) - happy
4. 穿 (chuān) - to wear, to put on
5. 衣服 (yīfú) - clothes
6. 旅館 (lǚguǎn) - hotel
7. 太太 (tàitai) - wife
8. 男孩子 (nán háizi) - boy, male child
9. 矮 (ǎi) - short (height)
10. 高 (gāo) - tall
11. 弟弟 (dìdi) - younger brother
12. 乾淨 (gānjìng) - clean
13. 窗戶 (chuānghù) - window
14. 往窗戶走去 (wǎng chuānghù zǒu qù) - walk towards the window

16. 因為...所以... (yīnwèi...suǒyǐ...) - because...therefore...

I. 看
kàn to try and see

Function: This pattern reduplicates a mono-syllabic action verb and ends with a cognitive verb 看. It suggests "try (verb) and see". Because of the use of 看, the sentence carries a highly tentative tone.

这杯咖啡很香，你喝喝看。
zhè bēi kāfēi hěn xiāng, nǐ hē hē kàn.
This cup of coffee smells good, why don't you take a sip?

听说你唱歌唱得很好，我想听听看。
tīng shuō nǐ chàng gē chàng dé hěn hǎo, wǒ xiǎng tīng tīng kàn.
I heard that you sing very well, I would like to listen and see.

那家餐厅的菜很好吃，我想去吃吃看。
nà jiā cāntīng de cài hěn hǎo chī, wǒ xiǎng qù chī chī kàn.
The food at that restaurant is delicious, I want to go and try it.

台湾的夜市很有名，这个周末我想去逛逛看。
Táiwān de yèshì hěn yǒumíng, zhège zhōumò wǒ xiǎng qù guàng guàng kàn.
The night markets in Taiwan are famous, I want to go and explore this weekend.

Usage:
1. In this lesson, we are focusing on a construction in which the reduplication of mono-syllabic verbs is followed by an attempt verb 看. Basic mono-syllabic action verbs can be used in this pattern, e.g., 吃 chī, 喝 hē, 打 dǎ, 写 xiě, 穿 chuān, 学 xué, 做 zuò, 听 tīng, 唱 chàng, 逛 guàng.
2. This pattern is closely related to the reduplication pattern introduced in Lesson 6. In most circumstances, they are interchangeable, e.g., 这杯咖啡很香，你喝喝看。vs. 这杯咖啡很香，你喝喝。"The coffee smells good. Take a sip." However, they are not interchangeable below.
(1) 我周末常在家看看书、喝喝咖啡、上上网。"I often spend my weekends reading, drinking coffee, and using the internet." Since the sentence is not used to ask someone to try something, "看" cannot be used.
(2) Generally speaking, the pattern "VV 看" cannot be followed by an object. You cannot say *喝喝看咖啡 However, the pattern of VV can be followed by an object, such as 吃吃饭、喝喝咖啡、帮帮我.Lesson 10: 台灣的水果很好吃。

IV. Change in Situation with Sentential 了 le m.
Function: The sentential 了 le indicates change situation, i.e., some change has taken place with a new situation resulting.
咖啡貴了。我會打綱球了。
現在有手機的人多了。我現在喜歡吃越南麵了。
Structures: The sentential 了 le appears at the very end of the sentence, which can be either affirmative or negative.

我媽媽不喝咖啡了。他不想買那支手機了。
我們不要去參觀故宮了。

Questions:
今天你想吃午餐了嗎？現在學中文的學生多了嗎？
你們不去臺束了嗎？

Goal: Learning to briefly explain and give reasons.
Task: Pair up with someone and hold discussions based on the following five questions. Share your conclusions with the class.

Báisè hónɡbāo

Zài Zhōnɡguó wénhuà lĭ，hěnduō rén rènwéi báisè biăozhŭn qīnhūnlĭ. Báisè biăoyŭ chéngrén de jiéhūn qúnzhōng，báisè de jiéhūn yīfu hé zhūshì dōu shì báisè de. Báisè biăoyŭ chéngrén de jiéhūn qúnzhōng，báisè de jiéhūn yīfu hé zhūshì dōu shì báisè de. Báisè hónɡbāo

Hóngsè niánhuí zhíjiē

Dāngdài Zhōnɡguó kèkè wò gěi xīnnián péi lǐ cái hóngbāo, lǐmiàn bǎocún qián, zhùfú tāmen huòdé hào yùn. Zhōnɡguó niánzhōnɡ, rénmen guà chū hónɡsè niánhuí zhíjiē hé duì联，hé zi "fú" 也写在红纸上带来好运。 Dàrén gěi háizi fàng qián de hónɡbāo.

Báisè hónɡbāoThe traditional royal color is yellow. The meaning of yellow has changed dramatically since ancient times. In imperial China, yellow was used exclusively by the emperor and the royal family. It was the color of the highest class. The robe worn by the emperor was called "黃袍" (huángpáo, literally "yellow gown"). Emperors and royal families no longer exist in modern China and the significance of the color yellow has undergone dramatic change. Today, it can mean "pornography" with the term "黃色書刊" (huángsè shūkān) meaning "pornographic books".雷代中文课程，我可以简单描述一个人的外貌。我可以描述食物的颜色、气味和味道。我可以简要解释并给出理由。我可以描述暂定的活动和情况的变化。第十一課：我想租房子

I. To Come to Do Something with lái / 来 (lái)
Function: '来 (lái) + VP' indicates the subject's intention of coming over to do something.
我来学中文。他来打篮球。
Structure: Negation markers, auxiliary verbs, or adverbs are placed before the first verbal element 来 (lái).

Negation:
我明天有事不来上课。
她不跟我来看电影。
我很忙，不来帮你装有线电视了。

Questions:
他不来吃晚饭吗？你们常来游泳吗？

Usage: The function of '来 (lái) + VP' in this lesson is the same as that of '去 (qù) + VP' in Lesson 3. The only difference is the direction of the subject's action, with 来 (lái) indicating towards and 去 (qù) indicating away from the speaker's location.

我星期四来/去上书法课。
我妹妹不想来/去吃牛肉面。

230Lesson: 我要租房子 (Wǒ yào zū fángzi)

III. Existential Subject with 有 (yǒu)
Function: 有 (yǒu) introduces the existence of an indefinite subject. The following VP in the sentence describes what the subject does.

0 有人住這裡。
0 有兩個學生來找你。
0 早上有一個小姐打電話給你。
昨天有一個先生來裝有線電視。
有一個人在外面唱歌。

Structures: The subject in Chinese is usually a definite noun. If the subject is indefinite, it needs to be preceded by 有 (yǒu).
Negation: 有 (yǒu) is always negated with 沒 (méi).

這間沒有人住。
沒有人要跟我去逛夜市。

IV. Different Types of 會 hui Usage: There are two different types of 會 hui. The first one, as presented in Lesson 5, refers to "acquired skills". The second one, in this lesson, refers to "possibility or likelihood".

他會做飯。 (hui4)
我不會打籃球。 (hui4)
我明天會去看看他。 (hui4)
他明天不會去上書法課。 (hui4)

II. Where I Live
Goal: Learning to talk about the environment of a room or house.
Task: Pair up with a classmate and describe your current residence or your residence back in your home country. As you listen to your partner, draw a floor plan of their house and label each room.

III. Story-telling
Goal: Learning to comprehend a passage and add things to it.
Task: Form groups of two or three. Read the following story and complete it with your partners. Read the completed story to the class. Evaluate each group's work.

李大同的女朋友昨天已經回國了。現在他一個人在家，他想，今天有一個很好看的棒球比賽，可是現在十一點半了，比賽已經結束了。他不知道要做什麼，所以想去看看他爸爸媽媽，他爸媽的家很近，走路五分鐘就到了。他打電話給他爸媽，他爸媽說，他們去旅行，不在家。現在，李大同不知道要做什麼...（請幫他想想吧！）

• I Would Like to Rent a Place
一
Renting a Place in Taiwan
乙；戶戸句正醞�之
. . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . .
Though it is possible to find rental apartments through real estate agents, in Taiwan, it is more common for landlords to rent their own places. Renting a place in Taiwan is very much a free market. In other words, while there are going prices for renting apartments, the final amount is determined by the landlord and it is possible to bargain the rent down. Therefore, it is best to shop around and haggle with the landlord to get a better price. Once an agreement is reached and written down on a lease, it has legal effect. Also in Taiwan, application fees or background screening fees are not necessary. However, the landlord might ask for a deposit of up to two months' rent, but prepayment of the final month's rent is not practiced.
－＂
房屋租赁流程

先再 Pattern:
Function: This pattern presents the temporal sequence of two consecutive events.
弟弟打算先去旅行再找工作。
我想先吃晚饭再给妈妈打电话。
他计划在台湾先学语言再念大学。

Usage: This pattern indicates the order of two events either in the past or future.
我昨天晚上先写功课，再看电视。
我明天先去图书馆看书，再去超市买食物。

II. To Focus with '/…
shi 的 de
是
Function: This pattern highlights one of the elements in a sentence in a past event and marks it as the focus/contrast, i.e., the main message of the sentence.
2531. 當代中文課程的結構是：在這個模式中，焦點標記詞「是」直接放在被聚焦的元素前面，而「的」則放在句子末尾，即主題聚焦。例如：他是昨天晚上到台灣的。他是在學校附近吃晚飯的。
2. 我是坐捷運來學校的。
3. 句子中的賓語通常移到句子最前面。例如：學費是公司替我付的。這支手機是在夜市買的。
4. 聚焦元素可以是主語、表示時間、地點、方式的表達，有時也可以是動詞，但從不是賓語。例如：是我打電話給房東的。我是昨天晚上去看電影的。他是在那家便利店買咖啡的。我是坐公車來上課的。但不包括賓語，例如：我是這間房間最近租的。
5. 否定詞「不」總是放在「是」之前。「他不是今天早上去美國的。不是我打電話給房東的。我不是在圖書館看書的。
6. 問句的結構是：你是哪個人來的嗎？他是坐高鐵去台南的嗎？你的房租是自己付的嗎？
7. 有時候「是」可以在「是...的」結構中省略。「我（是）跟朋友一起來的。我（是）坐計程車來的。」
8. 這種結構可以用來問過去事件的疑問詞（誰、什麼時候、如何、在哪裡），但對於「什麼」作為賓語時不適用。「誰打電話給你？」、「他是什麼時候來學校的？」LESSON • f 2 • 你在台灣學多久的中文？

Function: In this lesson, 以後y au is basically a noun but covers two different functions. In Dialogue I, it is used alone, just like a time word, meaning some time in the future. In Dialogue II, it is used together with two events, connecting them sequentially, i.e., after A, B.雷代中文課程

II. To Focus with 是 (shì) 的 (de)
Structures:
1. (1) It was last night that he arrived in Taiwan.
(2) It was near the school that he had dinner.
(3) It was by MRT that I came to school.

3. (1) It was I who called the landlord. (subject)
(2) It was last night that I went to see a movie. (time)
(3) It was in that convenience store that he bought coffee. (place)
(4) It was by taking the bus that I came to class. (manner)

Addressing People in the Workplace
Being polite at all times is viewed as important by the Chinese. The workplace is no exception. How people are addressed depends on many factors.

The most common way to address a person is by their job title. For example, a manager can be addressed as 王经理 Wáng Jīnglǐ "Manager Wang" or a professor as 李教授 Lǐ Jiàoshòu "Professor Li." People are also addressed by titles that indicate the highest level of education they received. For example, a person with a Ph.D. can be addressed as 陈博士 Chén Bóshì "Dr. Chen" or as 文学博士陈月文 Wénxué Bóshì Chén Yuèwén "Dr. of Literature Chen Yue-wen." Another method of address is based on profession, such as 张老师 Zhāng Lǎoshī "Teacher Zhang," or 王议员 Wáng Yìyuán "MP Wang" (MP = member of parliament). When one is unsure of someone's job title or profession, Miss 小姐 Xiǎojiě, Madam 女士 Nǚshì, or Mister 先生 Xiānshēng is also polite.

(Translation: Contemporary Chinese Course)LESSON • f 2 • 你在台灣學多久的中文？
Mow Long Will You Be Studying Chinese in Taiwan?

Privacy Means Something Different for Taiwanese.

Sometimes Taiwanese ask friends from abroad questions like "Where do you work?"; "How much do you make?"; "Are you married?"; "How many children do you have?"; and "Are they boys or girls?" While many foreigners consider these kinds of questions intrusive, in Taiwanese culture they are considered a sign of interest and a way of breaking the ice.

Happy Birthday!

在這一課中，我們將探討社交生活的重要性。學習如何與他人建立良好的關係，並在特殊場合中表現得體。Happy Birthday, An Tong. Yi Jun: Hey, how are you? An Tong: I'm good. Long time no see, I heard you went to Hualien? Yi Jun: I didn't go to Hualien, I just came back from Taiwan and Cambodia. An Tong: What's up? Why are you looking for me? Yi Jun: Tomorrow is your birthday, right? An Tong: Ah, how could I forget! I've been so busy lately. Thank you for remembering. Yi Jun: Of course I remember! During our language exchange, you were so enthusiastic about teaching me Spanish. An Tong: You're welcome, it's the same for you. Yi Jun: Tomorrow, I want to treat you to dinner and celebrate your birthday. 270安同和怡君：妳太客氣了，我們在哪裡見面呢？

安童：一军，谢谢你请我来这家有名的餐厅吃饭。
一军：不客气。不客气。这是我送给你的礼物。

一军：你想吃什么？有什么你不吃的吗？
安童：我什么都吃。
一军：我在来餐厅之前特别订了猪脚加细面线和蛋。等它们送过来就开始吧。
安童：台湾人过生日都吃这个吗？
一军：是的。这是传统，但现在大部分年轻人过生日不再吃这些东西了。
安童：那你们过生日都吃什么？
一军：我们也像你们一样吃蛋糕。我还订了一个生日蛋糕。
安童：你对我真好。
一军：生日快乐，安童。祝你万事如意，心想事成。
安童：谢谢！谢谢！Lesson: 生日快樂 (Shēngrì kuàilè)

Phrases:

In Lesson 13, we learn about negation in Chinese. There are two negative markers, 不 (bù) and 沒 (méi), which are used differently depending on the verb type.

A. Negation of action verbs:
1. 不 (bù) negation can have two interpretations:
(1) Habitual:
a. 我們星期六不上課。 (Wǒmen xīngqīliù bù shàngkè.) - We don't have classes on Saturdays.
b. 學生常不吃早餐。 (Xuéshēng cháng bù chī zǎocān.) - Students often don't eat breakfast.

Please note that the pinyin with tones has been added to the text for clarity.1. 当代中文课程的意图不是去图书馆，也不是找工作。
2. 昨天我没有给他打电话。
3. 上个星期我没有和同学去。
4. 今天我没有坐捷运来上课，我坐公车。
B. 状态动词的否定
1. 今天不热，我想出去逛逛。
2. 他说中文不难学，可是中国字不好写。
C. 我不舒服，今天不想出去。
否定过程动词
1. 中文课还没结束，所以我不能回国。
2. 我没忘。你先去学校，我等一下去找你。
3. 我还没决定要不要去旅行。

Usage: 在台湾，"没" 的否定比 "没有" 的否定更常见。例如："我没有买手机"。在中国大陆，"我没买手机" 更常见。

请简要说明为什么使用 "没" 或 "不" 在句子中，并且在空格处填入正确的汉字或拼音。

Explanation:
- "没" is used to negate process verbs, indicating non-happening.
- "不" is used to negate state verbs, indicating the contrary.
- In Taiwan, the negation "没" is more common than the negation "没有".Lesson: 生日快樂 (Shēngrì kuàilè) - Happy Birthday

Sentences:
1. 我覺得今天很好。(Wǒ juéde jīntiān hěn hǎo.) - I think today is great.
2. 昨天我和他去逛夜市。(Zuótiān wǒ hé tā qù guàng yèshì.) - Yesterday, I went to the night market with him.
3. 這家牛肉麵店很便宜。(Zhè jiā niúròu miàn diàn hěn piányí.) - This beef noodle restaurant is very cheap.
4. 比賽還沒開始，我先去買杯咖啡。(Bǐsài hái méi kāishǐ, wǒ xiān qù mǎi bēi kāfēi.) - The game hasn't started yet, so I'll go buy a cup of coffee first.

IV. All-inclusive with Question Words
Function: Question words can appear in declarative sentences in Chinese. When they do, they often co-occur with 都 (dōu) "all" to indicate totality without exception, that is, total inclusion in affirmative sentences and total exclusion in negative sentences.

Affirmative Negative Question
誰都喜歡去旅行。 (Shuí dōu xǐhuān qù lǚxíng.) - Everyone likes to travel.
哪裡都有好吃的食物。 (Nǎlǐ dōu yǒu hǎochī de shíwù.) - There is delicious food everywhere.
他什麼都想買。 (Tā shénme dōu xiǎng mǎi.) - He wants to buy everything.
弟弟什麼時候都在上網。 (Dìdi shénme shíhòu dōu zài shàngwǎng.) - My younger brother is always online.
他們學校很方便，怎麼去都能到。 (Tāmen xuéxiào hěn fāngbiàn, zěnme qù dōu néng dào.) - Their school is very convenient, you can get there no matter how you go.• 当代中文课程

在否定句中，疑问词与都(dōu)或也(yě)一起使用，表示完全排除。否定标记不(bù)或没(méi)放在都(dōu)或也(yě)之后。

V. More/Less ...Than Planned with 多 Verb
duō / shǎo rú shí
Function: Pre-verbal 多 duō "more" or 少 shǎo "less" indicates "more" or "less/fewer" than planned.

我最近没钱了，应该少买束西。
Wǒ zuìjìn méi qián le, yīnggāi shǎo mǎi shù xī.
I'm out of money recently, I should buy fewer things.

我中文不好，应该多看书，少看电视。
Wǒ zhōngwén bù hǎo, yīnggāi duō kànshū, shǎo kàn diànshì.
My Chinese is not good, I should read more books and watch less TV.

我们明天应该多穿衣服吗？
Wǒmen míngtiān yīnggāi duō chuān yīfu ma?
Should we wear more clothes tomorrow?

Usage: 一点 yīdiǎn "a little bit" is often used to modify the object. This pattern can refer to events in the past or in the future.

他喜欢台湾，想多学一点中文。
Tā xǐhuān Táiwān, xiǎng duō xué yīdiǎn zhōngwén.
He likes Taiwan and wants to learn a little bit of Chinese.

昨天我朋友来我家，我多做了一点菜。
Zuótiān wǒ péngyǒu lái wǒ jiā, wǒ duō zuò le yīdiǎn cài.
Yesterday my friend came to my house, and I cooked a little bit more food.

她今天太累了，想少做一点功课。
Tā jīntiān tài lèi le, xiǎng shǎo zuò yīdiǎn gōngkè.
She's too tired today and wants to do a little bit less homework.

VII. Comparison with ...一跟...樣 (yī gēn yàng)
IS IS

Function: This pattern is used to compare two people or things and indicate whether they are the same (equal) or not the same. The similar/same quality of the persons or things being compared, if any, follows 才羕.

這支手機跟那支手機樣。
Zhè zhī shǒujī gēn nà zhī shǒujī yàng.
This phone and that phone are the same.

我的生日跟她的生日樣，都是八月十七日。
Wǒ de shēngrì gēn tā de shēngrì yàng, dōu shì bā yuè shí qī rì.
My birthday and her birthday are the same, both on August 17th.

他跟我一樣，都常游泳。
Tā gēn wǒ yīyàng, dōu cháng yóuyǒng.
He is the same as me, we both often swim.

Structures: A 跟 B 樣 (state verb).

你點的菜跟我點的樣。
Nǐ diǎn de cài gēn wǒ diǎn de yàng.
The dish you ordered and the one I ordered are the same.

我跟我妹妹樣高。
Wǒ gēn wǒ mèimei yàng gāo.
I am the same height as my younger sister.

姐姐租的房子跟我租的樣貴。
Jiějie zū de fángzi gēn wǒ zū de yàng guì.
The house my older sister rented and the one I rented are equally expensive.

我跟我朋友樣喜歡看電視。
Wǒ gēn wǒ péngyǒu yàng xǐhuān kàn diànshì.
I and my friend both enjoy watching TV.

Negation:

不一樣 (bù yīyàng)
1. The negation 不 (bù) precedes 樣 (yīyàng) to indicate that the two nouns are different in quality.

中國茶跟日本茶不一樣。
Zhōngguó chá gēn Rìběn chá bù yīyàng.
Chinese tea and Japanese tea are not the same.

我跟妹妹不一樣高。
Wǒ gēn mèimei bù yīyàng gāo.
I am not as tall as my younger sister.

The negation marker 不 (bù) can also precede 跟 (gēn), but when it does, it negates the object to be compared with, i.e., the 跟 (gēn) part, not the "same" part.

他不跟我樣高，跟小王樣高。
Tā bù gēn wǒ yàng gāo, gēn xiǎo wáng yàng gāo.
He is not as tall as me, but he is as tall as Xiao Wang.

Questions:

是不是樣 (shì bù shì yàng)
To ask a question, the A-not-A pattern can be used with 樣 (yàng) or 是不是 (shì bù shì) can be placed in front of 樣 (yàng).

小籠包跟包子樣不樣？
Xiǎolóngbāo gēn bāozi yàng bù yàng?
Are xiaolongbao and baozi the same?

小籠包跟包子是不是樣？
Xiǎolóngbāo gēn bāozi shì bù shì yàng?
Are xiaolongbao and baozi the same?

今年的生意是不是跟去年的樣好？
Jīnnián de shēngyì shì bù shì gēn qùnián de yàng hǎo?
Is this year's business as good as last year's?

說中文跟寫中文是不是樣難？
Shuō Zhōngwén gēn xiě Zhōngwén shì bù shì yàng nán?
Is speaking Chinese as difficult as writing Chinese?當代中文課程 - Match the activities to the pictures on the chart below, then write sentences using the following words: 跟 (gēn) ...一樣 (yīyàng), 喜歡 (xǐhuān), 好吃 (hǎochī), 好喝 (hǎohē).

1. 否定：今天没吃午餐。我最近很忙，一星期都没看电视。昨天跟朋友去过生日，所以我没写功课。
2. 问句：弟弟吃了午餐没有？下个月的学费，他付了没有？今晚的篮球比赛开始了吗？

4. 否定 vs 没否定：

         a. 我们星期六不上课。
         b. 学生经常不吃早餐。

         b. 他不找工作。

Translation:
• Contemporary Chinese Course Structure:
1. Negation: I didn't eat lunch today. I have been very busy lately, haven't watched TV for a week. Yesterday, I went to celebrate my friend's birthday so I didn't do the homework.
2. Questions: Did little brother eat his lunch? Did he pay the tuition for next month? Has tonight's basketball game started yet?
3. Usage: The correct way to say it is "I didn't have dinner."
4. Negation vs 没 Negation:
   a. Function: Negation of action verbs
      (1) Habitual:
         a. We don't go to school on Saturdays.
         b. Students often don't eat breakfast.
      (2) Intention not to:
         a. I'm not going to go to the library.
         b. He's not looking for a job.
   b. Function: Negation of action verbs
      (1) I didn't call him yesterday.
      (2) I didn't go to KTV with classmates last week.
      (3) I didn't come to class by MRT today, I took a bus.13 •

B. Negation of state verbs B. Negation of state verbs
(1) 今天不热，我想出去逛逛。 (jīntiān bù rè, wǒ xiǎng chūqù guàngguàng.) It is not hot today. I'd like to go out and look around.
(2) 他说中文不难学，可是中文字符不好写。 (tā shuō zhōngwén bù nán xué, kěshì zhōngwén zì bù hǎo xiě.) He said Chinese is not difficult to learn, but Chinese characters are hard to write.
(3) 我不舒服，今天不想出去。 (wǒ bù shūfú, jīntiān bù xiǎng chūqù.) I don't feel well. I don't want to go out today.

C. Negation of process verbs C. Negation of process verbs
(1) 中文课还没结束，所以我不能回国。 (zhōngwén kè hái méi jiéshù, suǒyǐ wǒ bù néng huíguó.) My Chinese classes have not ended yet, so I can't go back to my country.
(2) 我没忘。你先去学习的，我等一下去找你。 (wǒ méi wàng. nǐ xiān qù xuéxí de, wǒ děng yīxià qù zhǎo nǐ.) I didn't forget. You go to school first and I will go see you later.
(3) 我还没决定要不要去旅行。 (wǒ hái méi juédìng yào bùyào qù lǚxíng.) I still have not decided whether to take a trip or not.

He and I are the same. We both swim often. (We are alike.)

虽然这道菜跟我做的一样贵。(Suīrán zhè dào cài gēn wǒ zuò de yīyàng guì.)
Although this dish is as expensive as the one I made.

我跟我妹妹一样高。(Wǒ gēn wǒ mèimei yīyàng gāo.)
I am as tall as my younger sister.

姐姐租的房子跟我租的一样贵。(Jiějie zū de fángzi gēn wǒ zū de yīyàng guì.)
The house that my older sister rents is as expensive as the one I rent.

我跟我的朋友一样喜欢看电视。(Wǒ gēn wǒ de péngyou yīyàng xǐhuān kàn diànshì.)
My friend and I are the same. We both enjoy watching TV.

Negation: 否定 (Fǒudìng)
1. (1) 中國茶跟日本茶不一樣。 (Zhōngguó chá gēn Rìběn chá bù yīyàng.) Chinese tea and Japanese tea are different.
   (2) 我跟妹妹不一樣高。 (Wǒ gēn mèimei bù yīyàng gāo.) My younger sister and I are not the same height.

II. How Do You Celebrate Your Birthday?
Goal: Learning to briefly compare different cultures.
Task: Pair up with someone and ask each other how birthdays are celebrated in each other's home country. Check each item that applies. When you are done, consolidate the answers with everyone in class and have a representative report the similarities and differences in the ways birthdays are celebrated in different countries.

LESSON • 生日快樂
Happy Birthday.

Congratulatory Expressions in Chinese:
Congratulatory expressions are used to congratulate people on special occasions. Chinese people value this in interpersonal relationships and like to express caring thoughts at the right place, at the right time, and for the right occasion. Most of these sayings are four-character expressions with fixed and auspicious meanings. The most all-purpose congratulatory expression is probably 萬事如意，心想事成 (wànshì rúyì, xīnxiǎng shìchéng) "I wish you all the best and that all your wishes come true."

A Common congratulatory expression:
Taiwanese Birthdays: Traditionally, Chinese people celebrate their birthdays based on the lunar calendar, but today, most people celebrate their birthdays according to the Gregorian calendar. It is a tradition for babies to have a celebration called "抓周" (zhuā zhōu) at their first year of age.

蕙風堂／提供• 當代中文課程
Birthdays are very important to the Taiwanese and are celebrated according to the Gregorian calendar. Celebrations for infants are held when they are one-month and one-year old. Major decades, such as 60, 70, and 80 years of age, hold particular significance. The ancient tradition of 抓週 zhāozhōu (grabbing at the first year) is still practiced. For this custom, a child is surrounded by a number of items on their first birthday. The item that they grab is said to indicate their future character and profession.

Minghua: Ruyu, as heavy as it's raining, why didn't you bring an umbrella?
Ruyu: I brought it yesterday, but I forgot to bring it today.
Minghua: A typhoon is coming.
Ruyu: Yes, I've heard.
Minghua: We have typhoons every summer. When typhoons hit, we get heavy wind and rain. It gets very inconvenient to do anything.
Ruyu: Yeah. It gets wet everywhere. I hate it.
Minghua: The TV news says this typhoon is bigger than the last one and advised everyone to be extra cautious.
Ruyu: I hope the one this time is not as scary as the last one.
Minghua: Ruyu, Look. The rain has stopped.
Ruyu: Great! Thank you for the umbrella. See you.
Minghua: You're welcome. Take care.

IV.
Comparison 更 gèng even more so
Function: The adverb 更 presents a fact that is superior to a fact presented in a previous statement. E.g., 星期天我更忙。Xīngqítiān wǒ gèng máng means that I am/will be even busier on Sunday than normally. In this lesson, we will introduce sentences in which 更 is used with 比 comparison.

他很高，他哥哥比他更高。
今年比去年更冷。
我觉得芒果比西瓜更好吃。

Structures: 更 is an adverb that modifies state verbs and is thus placed in front of state verbs.

Questions: The 是不 pattern is typically used in this structure.

这次的台风是不是比上次的更大？
在学校上网是不是比在家里更快？

309• 當代中文課程

Inferior Comparison 沒有 meiyou
The pattern "A沒有B那麼／這麼…" is used to compare two things A & B and is used to indicate that A is not as (adjective) as B.

哥哥沒有爸爸那麼高。
火車沒有高鐵那麼快。

我的中文沒有老師的那麼好。
臭豆腐沒有牛肉麵這麼好吃。
甜點沒有小籠包那麼好做。
這次的颱風沒有上次的那麼可怕。

Structures: Note that this pattern is usually used in the negative, 沒（有）mei(you). Sometimes, 那麼name or 這麼zheme can be omitted. Its positive counterpart, "A有you B那麼name/這麼zheme state verb", is rarely used, except in 嗎 questions.14•
LESSON • 天氣這麼冷 ！
It's So Cold!
Questions: The A-not-A pattern is used for questions.
妹妹有沒有哥哥那麼漂亮？
Does younger sister look as pretty as older brother?
花蓮的房租有沒有台北的那麼貴？
Is the rent in Hualien as expensive as in Taipei?
日本的工作有沒有美國的那麼難找？
Is it as difficult to find a job in Japan as it is in the United States?
夏天的天氣有沒有春天的舒服？
Is the weather in summer as comfortable as in spring?

Usage: This pattern indicates that A is not as (adjective) as B. When A and B are the same, use the "equal degree" pattern introduced in Lesson 13, 'A 跟 gen B ­…比樣yiyaOng…'. The pattern for "superior degree", 'A bzB ' was introduced in Lesson 8. When you ask a question like 今天有沒有昨天熱? Is today as hot as yesterday? It is assumed that yesterday was quite hot. Three different responses to the question are possible as shown below:
(equal degree)
今天跟昨天一樣熱。
Today is equally hot compared to yesterday.
(inferior degree)
今天沒有昨天那麼熱。
Today is not as hot as yesterday.
(superior degree)
今天比昨夭熱。
Today is hotter than yesterday.

Answer the questions given using the A 沒有 B 那麼 ／ 這麼… pattern.

哥哥和弟弟，誰比較高？哥哥沒有弟弟那麼高。
Between older brother and younger brother, who is taller? Older brother is not as tall as younger brother.

台北和紐約，哪裡比較冷？
Between Taipei and New York, which place is colder?

西瓜和芒果，哪種水果比較甜？
Between watermelon and mango, which fruit is sweeter?

今年的生意好還是去年的好？
Is business better this year or last year?

咖啡好喝，還是烏龍茶好喝？

- 旅行。當代中文課程《當代中文課程》是一個關於台風假期的話題。所謂「台風假期」是指在預計未來四小時內，有望通過某個地區的風速達到7級或更高，或陣風達到10級或更高時，宣布學校和工作停止直到風暴過去。 台風帶來強風和大雨，決定是否取消工作和上學的權力由人事行政總局掌握。1993年，人事行政總局考慮了中央氣象局的天氣預報和地方政府的建議後，決定是否宣布全國性的台風假期。如今，這一決策已轉交給地方政府。要了解是否因為颱風而停止工作和上學，可以查看當地新聞或人事行政總局官方網站http://www.cpa.gov.tw/ 或致電020-300-166查詢最新消息。天气这么冷！

I. Non-committal Stance with Question Words

哪裡 (nǎlǐ) - Where

頑 (wán) - stubborn

Function: When question words (e.g., 什麼 shénme, 多少 duōshǎo, 幾 jǐ, 什麼地方 shénme dìfāng, 誰 shéi zài shénme shíhòu) occur in a declarative sentence, the sentence indicates a non-committal attitude on the part of the speaker who is avoiding giving a clear answer. Non-committal statements are always in the negative.

我沒有多少錢。她沒有幾個朋友。

你的威冒沒有什麼關係。我沒去哪裡。

他不打算買什麼。我昨天沒跟誰去看電影。

Answer the question using question words indicating a non-committal attitude.

你的房租一個月多少錢？沒有多少錢。

週末快到了，你打算去哪裡玩？我不知道。

你在看什麼？我不知道。

你在台灣有很多朋友嗎？我不知道。

你昨天去便利店買了什麼？我昨天沒去。

3311. 當代中文課程 - 當代中文課程 (dāng dài zhōng wén kè chéng)
II. To Dispose of Something with 把 ba - 使用把字句處理物品 (shǐ yòng bǎ zì jù chǔ lǐ wù pǐn)
Function: This pattern is generally referred to as 才巴 ba or disposal construction. It consists of a variety of internal elements and is quite similar to the phrase "take this (noun) and..." in English, but much more widely used. We begin with the most basic structure, which refers to how a noun, object of the action verb, is disposed of by the subject.
我把牛肉麵吃了。他把我的湯喝了。
房間把房子賣了。
Structures: 把 ba + object + verb 十 了 le, where the object is most cases definite in reference (bare nouns or nouns with modifiers such as 這個，那個，他的 etc.), the verb (bare, i.e., just one character) must be an outward transitive action verb (action away from the actor, not inward towards the actor), and sentence must end with the particle 了．
Negation: The negation uses 沒 or 別 occurs in front of the particle 把 ba.
我沒把豬腳麵線吃了。別把我的筆吃了。
他沒把書賣了。
Questions:
你把功課寫了沒有? 你是不是把機車賣了？
你是不是把他的早飯吃了？
Usage:
(1) As mentioned above, the object of 把 ba must be definite.
(2) 我想把手機賣了。
我想把那支手機賣了。
2. ＊我想把一支手機賣了。
As also mentioned earlier, the bare verb in 把 ba sentences must be outward and transitive. They include 賣 mài, 吃 chī, 喝 hē, 寫 xiě but not such inward verbs as 買 mǎi, 學 xué. You cannot say *我把中文學了．Lesson 5: 我很不舒服 (wǒ hěn bù shūfú) - I feel very uncomfortable.

1. The notion "dispose of" is often indicated using "do-with", "do-to", and "take (noun) and (verb)" in English, e.g., "What he did with his car was to sell it" or "He took his car and sold it."

III. V /

...

了 (le) 就 (jiù) - right after doing...

Function: The pattern V 了...就... indicates that event 2 occurs right after the completion of event 1.

我放了假就去旅行。他吃了饭就睡觉。

爸爸回了家就喝了两杯乌龙茶。

Structures: The two events can be in the affirmative or negative.

他到了台北，就去台北101看看。

妹妹喝了一碗热汤，就不觉得冷了。

姐姐吃了臭豆腐，肚子就不舒服。• 當代中文課程

-!;,

The A-not-A form is not possible. Either 嗎 má or 是不是 shìbùshì can be used to form questions.

他們見了面，就去喝咖啡嗎？
Nǐ dìdì shì bù shì xiàle kè, jiù qù KTV chànggē?
Tā shì bù shì qù Niǔyuē wánle liǎng gè xīngqí, jiù bù xiǎng huílái?

Usage: The "V 了 …就…" pattern taught in this lesson is similar to the " -…就" in Lesson 13, but differs as explained below:

1. The " - " is followed by a relatively short verbal phrase, e.g., 出來就…
and 看就…, to emphasize the immediate succession of the two actions. In contrast, the "V 了" pattern is not as restricted in terms of what can follow it.

2. "以後" can be used with "V 了 …就…", but it cannot with the "-…就" pattern.

他吃了晚飯以後，就去睡覺。
＊他一吃了晚飯以後，就去睡覺。

IV. -點 yidi訕 a bit
一
．
Function: The combination 點 yidian indicates a minimal quantity or degree.
他喝了一點咖啡。
這一點錢太少了。
她要吃一點麵線。
一
Structures: 點 yidian can appear in a variety of structures as illustrated below.
一
1. (1點) 十 NP: Before a noun as its modifier. (2)
她在超市買了一點東西。我只喝了一點烏龍茶。
2. 昨天下了一點雨。
Vs + -點 ： After a state verb as its modifier, it indicates comparison, as in "a little more/less…".
他比我年輕一點。請你早一點來！明天我會晚-點回家。
3 有 （ ） 點 十 Vs: Before a state verb but preceded by 有 as a modifier of the adjective, it doesn't indicate comparison.
牛肉麵有-點辣。這裡，冬天有-點冷。
這支手機有-點貴。他有（一）點想睡。
Usage: 點 can be reduplicated to form 點點， indicating that something is "just a tiny bit", e.g., 我只要 點點。zhr y沁 yidiandian. "I just want a little bit."
Complete the sentences below using the minimal quantity expression 點．

B: 我只（喝湯）。

Pattern 2 above is used most frequently.
比 (Bǐ)
Comparison: The negation marker 不 (bù) precedes.

他做飯不比我做得快。(Tā zuò fàn bù bǐ wǒ zuò dé kuài.)
He doesn't cook faster than me.

走路，我不比他走得快。(Zǒulù, wǒ bù bǐ tā zǒu dé kuài.)
Walking, I don't walk faster than him.

弟弟念書念得不比哥哥好。(Dìdi niànshū niàn dé bù bǐ gēgē hǎo.)
Younger brother studies, but not better than older brother.

It snowed for three and a half months this year. It snowed less than last year.

Last weekend, I sang at K'IV for five hours. This weekend, I sang at K'IV for four hours.

Mom walks very fast. It takes twenty minutes from home to the subway station. Not faster than sister, who only takes ten minutes.• 當代中文課程
VI. Complements of Degree in Comparison Structures
Function: Degrees can be presented either as a pre-verbal adverbial or as a post-verbal complement. In this lesson, we focus on the latter type, using 點 yīdiǎn, 得 duō, and 多 le.
他的房間比我的大一點。
捷運站比公車站遠得多。
我覺得晚上比早上舒服多了。
Questions:
Structures:
1. 哥哥是不是比弟弟高一點？
2. 房租可以便宜一點嗎？
3. 春天去旅行是不是比夏天舒服得多？
4. 高鐵票比火車票貴多了嗎？

Answer the questions below using 點 yīdiǎn, 得 duō, and 多 le in the complements.

問 Ask 答 Answer
1. 高鐵比公車快嗎？高鐵比公車快得多／快多了。
2. 西瓜比芒果大嗎？
3. 安同和田中誰打籃球打得好？（安同）
4. 便利商店的東西貴還是超市的貴？
5. 姐姐和妹妹誰玩得開心？（妹妹）

VII. Separable Verbs
Function: This is a special category of verbs. The inherent structure of most separable verbs is [V+N]. The V and N can be separated, and an element can be inserted between them. The separated V and N behave like a verb and object. Examples of separable verbs are:

唱歌 (chànggē) - to sing
上班 (shàngbān) - to go to work
上綱 (shànggāng) - to set the main points
上課 (shàngkè) - to attend class
生病 (shēngbìng) - to get sick
睡覺 (shuìjiào) - to sleep
看書 (kànshū) - to read books
念書 (niànshū) - to study books
滑雪 (huáxuě) - to ski
潜泳 (qiányǒng) - to dive
照相 (zhàoxiàng) - to take photos
吃飯 (chīfàn) - to eat meals
做飯 (zuòfàn) - to cook meals
見面(jiànmiàn)-to meet

Structures: Basically, there are three types of separable forms. Let's take the words introduced in this volume as examples.

(1)
1. 了 inserted. The 了 is the Verbal 了 here.
(2)
他回家以後，就開始工作。
Tā huí jiā yǐhòu, jiù kāishǐ gōngzuò.
After he returned home, he started working.

2. 我昨天下課就跟朋友去看電影。
Wǒ zuótiān xiàkè jiù gēn péngyǒu qù kàn diànyǐng.
I went to watch a movie with my friends right after class yesterday.

(1)
Object inserted. Object refers to the recipient of an action.
(2)
我想見你一面。
Wǒ xiǎng jiàn nǐ yīmiàn.
I want to meet you.

他照了你一張相。
Tā zhào le nǐ yī zhāng xiàng.
He took a photo of you.

3. Time-Duration inserted.

－(3)

他唱了三小時的歌，有點累。
Tā chàng le sān xiǎoshí de gē, yǒudiǎn lèi.
He sang for three hours and feels a bit tired.

3. 一点 (yīdiǎn) - a bit
4. 附近的咖啡店有一点儿人。(Fùjìn de kāfēi diàn yǒu yīdiǎn rén.) - The coffee shop nearby has a few people.
5. 这一点钱太少了。(Zhè yīdiǎn qián tài shǎo le.) - This amount of money is too little.
6. 她想吃一点细面。(Tā xiǎng chī yīdiǎn xì miàn.) - She wants to eat a little bit of fine noodles.
7. 她只喝了一点乌龙茶。(Tā zhǐ hēle yīdiǎn wūlóngchá.) - She only drank a little Oolong tea.
8. 昨天下了一点雨。(Zuótiān xiàle yīdiǎn yǔ.) - It rained a little yesterday.
9. 他比我年轻一点。(Tā bǐ wǒ niánqīng yīdiǎn.) - He is a little bit younger than I am.
10. 请你早一点来！(Qǐng nǐ zǎo yīdiǎn lái!) - Please arrive a little early!
11. 明天我会晚一点回家。(Míngtiān wǒ huì wǎn yīdiǎn huíjiā.) - I'll be home a little later tomorrow.
12. 牛肉面有一点辣。(Niúròu miàn yǒu yīdiǎn là.) - The beef noodles is a little spicy.
13. 这里，冬天有一点冷。(Zhèlǐ, dōngtiān yǒu yīdiǎn lěng.) - Here, the winters are a bit cold.
14. 这部手机有一点贵。(Zhè bù shǒujī yǒu yīdiǎn guì.) - This cell phone is a little expensive.
15. 他有点儿想睡。(Tā yǒudiǎnr xiǎng shuì.) - He is a little sleepy.
16. 哥哥吃牛肉面比弟弟多。(Gēgē chī niúròu miàn bǐ dìdì duō.) - Older brother eats more beef noodles than the younger brother.
17. 这种手机卖得比那种好。(Zhè zhǒng shǒujī mài de bǐ nà zhǒng hǎo.) - This type of cell phone sells better than that type.
18. 他比我做得快。(Tā bǐ wǒ zuò de kuài.) - He does it faster than I do.
19. 我比他走得快。(Wǒ bǐ tā zǒu de kuài.) - I walk faster than he does.
20. 弟弟比哥哥你读得好。(Dìdì bǐ gēgē nǐ dú de hǎo.) - The younger brother studies better than his older brother.Lesson: 我很不舒服。I don't feel well.

Complements of Degree in Comparison Structures:
他的房间比我的大一点。Tā de fángjiān bǐ wǒ de dà yīdiǎn. His room is just a little bigger than mine.
捷运站比公车站远很多。Jiéyùnzhàn bǐ gōngchēzhàn yuǎn hěn duō. The MRT station is much farther away than the bus stop.
我觉得晚上比早上舒服多了。Wǒ juéde wǎnshàng bǐ zǎoshang shūfu duōle. I think evenings are a lot more comfortable than mornings.

9· 348LEI Doesn't Often Wear Well 我很不舒服 (Wǒ hěn bù shūfú)
Wearing Surgical Masks
You see people wearing surgical masks. Are they ill? Probably not. People in Taiwan wear surgical masks as a preventative measure among other reasons.
When the seasons are changing, it is easy to catch a cold and since colds are transmitted via the respiratory system, wearing a mask on crowded public buses or the MRT can help prevent transmission.
During the winter months, people on scooters wear masks to stay warm and also to filter out air pollution. Servers in restaurants wear masks to keep particles from unintentionally landing in food. Hospital workers and patients wear masks to prevent viral infections. People often wear surgical masks to help stay healthy and help prevent transmission of diseases.
小MRT
A Wearing surgical masks in stations "'- Wearing surgical masks in the hospital
